return h*60+m\n    b=pd.read_csv('production_batches.csv'); q=pd.read_csv('quality_inspections.csv'); log=pd.read_csv('machine_assignment_log.csv'); prod=pd.read_csv('products.csv'); wo=pd.read_csv('maintenance_work_orders.csv')\n    log['start_min']=log.start_time.map(minutes); log['prod_ts']=(log.day-1)*1440+log.start_min\n    rows=[]\n    for _,r in wo.iterrows():\n        d={}\n        for line in pathlib.Path(r.report_path).read_text().splitlines():\n            if ':' in line:\n                k,v=line.split(':',1);
